                <span id="foas"><div class="row odd "><h4 class="program_title">Unemployment Insurance</h4><p class="agency"><strong>Managing Agency: </strong>U.S. Department of Labor</p><div class="program_description_intro"><strong>Program Description: </strong>Unemployment insurance (UI) benefits give temporary financial help to eligible workers. Each state, as well as the District of Columbia, the Virgin Islands, and Puerto... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Unemployment Insurance" data-agency="U.S. Department of Labor">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>Unemployment insurance (UI) benefits give temporary financial help to eligible workers. Each state, as well as the District of Columbia, the Virgin Islands, and Puerto Rico, has UI programs.</p>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p><strong>Can I get unemployment insurance benefits?</strong></p>

<p>To qualify for unemployment benefits you must meet both of the conditions below:</p>

<ol>
	<li>You must have worked a one-year base period within the past 1215 months. You must also have earned enough wages to qualify for benefits, and</li>
	<li>You must be unemployed through no fault of your own and meet other state eligibility requirements.</li>
</ol>

<p>To learn more, visit the U.S. Department of Labors <a href="http://workforcesecurity.doleta.gov/unemploy/uifactsheet.asp" target="_blank">State Unemployment Insurance Benefits</a> page.</p>
<p><strong>Application Process</strong></p><p><strong>How do I file a claim?</strong></p>

<p>To apply for benefits, contact your states UI agency to file a claim as soon as possible after you become unemployed. You can use CareerOneStops <a href="http://www.servicelocator.org/UI_Filing_Assistance.asp" target="_blank">Unemployment Benefits Finder</a> to find your states agency. Benefits vary by state.</p>

<p>In some states, you can file a claim online or by phone.</p>
<p><strong>Program Contact Information</strong></p><p>If you have questions, please call the Employment and Training Helpline for more details.</p>

<ul>
	<li>1-877-US2-JOBS (1-877-872-5627)</li>
	<li>TTY 1-877-889-5627</li>
</ul>
<a class="read_less" href="javascript:void(0);">Read Less</a></div></div><div class="row even "><h4 class="program_title">Emergency Conservation Program (ECP) for Agricultural Producers</h4><p class="agency"><strong>Managing Agency: </strong>U.S. Department of Agriculture</p><div class="program_description_intro"><strong>Program Description: </strong>The Emergency Conservation Program (ECP) offers funding and assistance to farmers and ranchers to repair damage to farmlands caused by natural disasters. It also helps to... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Emergency Conservation Program (ECP) for Agricultural Producers" data-agency="U.S. Department of Agriculture">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>The Emergency Conservation Program (ECP) offers funding and assistance to farmers and ranchers to repair damage to farmlands caused by natural disasters. It also helps to put water conservation methods in place for times of severe drought and can help pay for their installation.</p>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p>For your land to qualify for funds, the damage must create new conservation problems that, if not dealt with, would:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Further damage the land.</li>
	<li>Greatly affect the lands productive capacity.</li>
	<li>Represent natural disaster damage that is unusual for the area (except damage from wind erosion).</li>
	<li>Be too costly of a repair to return the land to production without federal help.</li>
</ul>

<p>The FSA County Committee inspects the damage to determine if your land qualifies for ECP. Conservation problems that existed before the disaster or severe drought are not eligible.</p>

<p>To rehabilitate farmland, you may carry out emergency conservation actions like:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Remove debris from farmland.</li>
	<li>Restore livestock dung and conservation structures.</li>
	<li>Provide water for livestock during periods of severe drought.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Application Process</strong></p><p>Check with your local FSA office to find out about ECP sign-up periods. The FSA County Committee sets the sign-up periods.</p>

<p>To apply, contact your local <a href="http://offices.sc.egov.usda.gov/locator/app" target="_blank">USDA Service Center</a>.</p>
<p><strong>Program Contact Information</strong></p><p>To learn more, please visit the <a href="http://www.fsa.usda.gov/programs-and-services/conservation-programs/emergency-conservation/index" target="_blank">Emergency Conservation Program</a> page.</p>
<a class="read_less" href="javascript:void(0);">Read Less</a></div></div><div class="row odd "><h4 class="program_title">Farm Operating Loans (Direct and Guaranteed)</h4><p class="agency"><strong>Managing Agency: </strong>U.S. Department of Agriculture</p><div class="program_description_intro"><strong>Program Description: </strong>The Farm Service Agency (FSA) offers farm operating loans, both direct and guaranteed, to family farmers and ranchers. These loans can help those who are temporarily... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Farm Operating Loans (Direct and Guaranteed)" data-agency="U.S. Department of Agriculture">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>The Farm Service Agency (FSA) offers farm operating loans, both direct and guaranteed, to family farmers and ranchers. These loans can help those who are temporarily unable to get private, commercial credit on their own at reasonable rates and terms.</p>

<p>Operating Loans may be used to:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Buy items like livestock and feed, farm equipment, fuel, farm chemicals, and insurance.</li>
	<li>Pay family living expenses and other operating costs.</li>
	<li>Make minor improvements or repairs to buildings and fencing.</li>
	<li>Refinance certain farm-related debt, except real estate.</li>
</ul>

<p>FSA also offers Microloans. These are direct operating loans with a shortened application process and reduced paperwork. These loans meet the needs of smaller, non-traditional, and niche-type operations. Visit the <a href="http://www.fsa.usda.gov/programs-and-services/farm-loan-programs/microloans/index" target="_blank">Microloans Program</a> page for more details.</p>

<p>The maximum loan amount for a Direct Operating Loan is $300,000. The maximum for a Microloan is $50,000. No down payment is required; other terms and conditions apply. Visit the <a href="http://www.fsa.usda.gov/programs-and-services/farm-loan-programs/farm-operating-loans/index" target="_blank">Farm Operating Loans</a> page for more details.</p>

<p>Under an FSA guaranteed loan, you apply to an agricultural lender. The lender makes and services the loan, and FSA guarantees it against loss up to a maximum of 95 percent. The FSA guarantee permits lenders to offer credit to farmers who dont meet the normal criteria; certain terms and conditions apply. Visit the <a href="http://www.fsa.usda.gov/programs-and-services/farm-loan-programs/guaranteed-farm-loans/index" target="_blank">Guaranteed Farm Loans</a> page for more details.</p>

<p>The maximum loan amount for a Guaranteed Operating Loan is $1,399,000.</p>

<p>FSAs mission is not just to provide creditits to provide supervised credit. This means FSA works with you to identify strengths and opportunities for improvement in your farming operation. You can learn better business and financial planning that may help guide you toward success.</p>

<p>The goal of FSAs farm loan programs is to help you get to commercial credit in the future. Once you, as a farmer, are able to get credit from a commercial lender on your own, the agencys mission is complete.</p>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p>To qualify, you must meet all loan requirements, including those below; other terms and conditions apply:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Be a family farmer.</li>
	<li>Have a satisfactory credit history.</li>
	<li>For direct loans only, show sufficient farm management experience through education, training, or at least one year of farm experience (managing or operating) within the last five years.</li>
	<li>Be a U.S. citizen, non-citizen national, or legal resident alien. This includes Puerto Rico, the U.S. Virgin Islands, Guam, American Samoa, and certain former Pacific Trust Territories.</li>
	<li>Be unable to get credit elsewhere at reasonable rates and terms to meet actual needs.</li>
	<li>Be able to take on legal loan obligations.</li>
	<li>Have no overdue federal debt and have caused no FSA loss through debt forgiveness (certain exceptions apply), and</li>
	<li>Be the operator of the family farm after loan closing.</li>
</ul>

<p>Visit the <a href="http://www.fsa.usda.gov/dafl" target="_blank">Farm Loan Programs</a> page to learn more about the different FSA loan programs or you may also contact FSA directly.</p>
<p><strong>Application Process</strong></p><p>To apply for a Direct Farm Operating Loan, you must complete form <a href="http://forms.sc.egov.usda.gov/efcommon/eFileServices/eForms/FSA2001.PDF" target="_blank">FSA-2001, Request for Direct Loan Assistance</a> (PDF, 586 KB). Submit this form and all required documentation to your local USDA Service Center or FSA County Office.</p>

<p>Please read the <a href="http://www.fsa.usda.gov/Internet/FSA_File/loanapp13.pdf" target="_blank">How to Complete an FSA Loan Application</a> (PDF, 164 KB) fact sheet to learn more about the process.</p>

<p>To apply for a guaranteed loan, talk with your lender. They will make the arrangements.</p>
<p><strong>Program Contact Information</strong></p><p>Use the <a href="http://offices.sc.egov.usda.gov/locator/app" target="_blank">USDA Service Center Locator</a> to find and contact your local Service Center or FSA County Office to learn more.</p>
<a class="read_less" href="javascript:void(0);">Read Less</a></div></div><div class="row even "><h4 class="program_title">Farm Ownership Loans (Direct and Guaranteed)</h4><p class="agency"><strong>Managing Agency: </strong>U.S. Department of Agriculture</p><div class="program_description_intro"><strong>Program Description: </strong>The Farm Service Agency (FSA) offers farm ownership loans, both direct and guaranteed, to family farmers and ranchers. These loans can help those who are temporarily... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Farm Ownership Loans (Direct and Guaranteed)" data-agency="U.S. Department of Agriculture">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>The Farm Service Agency (FSA) offers farm ownership loans, both direct and guaranteed, to family farmers and ranchers. These loans can help those who are temporarily unable to get private, commercial credit on their own at reasonable rates and terms.</p>

<p>Farm Ownership Loans may be used to:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Buy or expand an existing farm.</li>
	<li>Build new or improve existing farm structures.</li>
	<li>Pay closing costs.</li>
	<li>Pay for soil and water conservation and protection.</li>
	<li>Refinance certain farm-related debt.</li>
</ul>

<p>The maximum loan amount for a Direct Farm Ownership Loan is $300,000. No down payment is required; other terms and conditions apply. Visit the <a href="http://www.fsa.usda.gov/programs-and-services/farm-loan-programs/farm-ownership-loans/index" target="_blank">Farm Ownership Loans</a> page for more details.</p>

<p>Under an FSA guaranteed loan, you apply to an agricultural lender. The lender makes and services the loan, and FSA guarantees it against loss up to a maximum of 95 percent. The FSA guarantee permits lenders to offer credit to farmers who dont meet the normal criteria; certain terms and conditions apply. Visit the <a href="http://www.fsa.usda.gov/programs-and-services/farm-loan-programs/guaranteed-farm-loans/index" target="_blank">Guaranteed Farm Loans</a> page for more details.</p>

<p>The maximum loan amount for a Guaranteed Farm Ownership Loan is $1,399,000.</p>

<p>FSAs mission is not just to provide creditits to provide supervised credit. This means FSA works with you to identify strengths and opportunities for improvement in your farming operation. You can learn better business and financial planning that may help guide you toward success.</p>

<p>The goal of FSAs farm loan programs is to help you get to commercial credit in the future. Once you, as a farmer, are able to get credit from a commercial lender on your own, the agencys mission is complete.</p>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p>To qualify, you must meet all loan requirements, including those below; other terms and conditions apply:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Be a family farmer.</li>
	<li>Have a satisfactory credit history.</li>
	<li>For direct loans, have taken part in the business operations of a farm for at least three out of the prior 10 years.</li>
	<li>Be a U.S. citizen, non-citizen national, or legal resident alien. This includes Puerto Rico, the U.S. Virgin Islands, Guam, American Samoa, and certain former Pacific Trust Territories.</li>
	<li>Be unable to get credit elsewhere at reasonable rates and terms to meet actual needs.</li>
	<li>Have legal capacity to take on loan obligations.</li>
	<li>Have no overdue federal debt and have caused no FSA loss through debt forgiveness (certain exceptions apply), and</li>
	<li>Be the owner-operator of the family farm after loan closing.</li>
</ul>

<p>Visit the <a href="http://www.fsa.usda.gov/programs-and-services/farm-loan-programs/index" target="_blank">Farm Loan Programs</a> page to learn more about the different FSA loan programs or contact FSA directly.</p>
<p><strong>Application Process</strong></p><p>To apply for a Direct Farm Ownership Loan, you must complete application form <a href="http://forms.sc.egov.usda.gov/efcommon/eFileServices/eForms/FSA2001.PDF" target="_blank">FSA-2001, Request for Direct Loan Assistance</a> (PDF, 586 KB). Submit this form and all required documentation to your local USDA Service Center or FSA County Office.</p>

<p>Please read the <a href="http://www.fsa.usda.gov/Internet/FSA_File/loanapp13.pdf" target="_blank">How to Complete an FSA Loan Application</a> (PDF, 164 KB) fact sheet to learn more about the process.</p>

<p>To apply for a guaranteed loan, talk with your lender. They will make the arrangements.</p>
<p><strong>Program Contact Information</strong></p><p>Use the <a href="http://offices.sc.egov.usda.gov/locator/app" target="_blank">USDA Service Center Locator</a> to find and contact your local Service Center or FSA County Office to learn more.</p>
<a class="read_less" href="javascript:void(0);">Read Less</a></div></div><div class="row odd "><h4 class="program_title">Noninsured Crop Disaster Assistance Program</h4><p class="agency"><strong>Managing Agency: </strong>U.S. Department of Agriculture</p><div class="program_description_intro"><strong>Program Description: </strong>The U.S. Department of Agriculture's Farm Service Agency's (USDA FSA) Noninsured Crop Disaster Assistance Program (NAP) offers payments to producers of eligible crops to... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Noninsured Crop Disaster Assistance Program" data-agency="U.S. Department of Agriculture">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>The U.S. Department of Agriculture's Farm Service Agency's (USDA FSA) Noninsured Crop Disaster Assistance Program (NAP) offers payments to producers of eligible crops to protect against low yields, loss of inventory, or prevented planting due to a natural disaster.</p>

<p>Visit the <a href="http://www.fsa.usda.gov/programs-and-services/disaster-assistance-program/noninsured-crop-disaster-assistance/index" target="_blank">NAP</a> page to get more details.</p>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p>You may qualify if youre a landowner, tenant, or sharecropper who shares in the risk of producing an eligible crop. You must be entitled to an ownership share of that crop. To qualify per the Agricultural Act of 2014, your average adjusted gross income (AGI) limitation cannot exceed $900,000. Other terms and conditions also apply.</p>

<p>Your crops must be commercially produced, agricultural commodities for which crop insurance is not available.</p>

<p>Eligible crops may be any of the following:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Grown for food.</li>
	<li>Planted and grown for livestock use, like grain and forage crops, and native forage.</li>
	<li>Grown for fiber, like cotton and flax (except trees).</li>
	<li>Grown in a controlled environment, like mushrooms and floriculture.</li>
	<li>Specialty crops, like honey and maple sap.</li>
	<li>Sea oats and sea grass.</li>
	<li>Sweet sorghum and biomass sorghum.</li>
	<li>Industrial crops, including those used in manufacturing or as feedstock for renewable or bio-based products.</li>
	<li>Value loss crops, such as aquaculture, Christmas trees, ginseng, ornamental nursery and turf-grass sod.</li>
	<li>Seed crops with stock produced for sale as seed stock for other eligible NAP crop production.</li>
</ul>

<p>You must contact a crop insurance agent with questions about insurability of a crop in your county. To learn which crops qualify for NAP coverage, you must contact the FSA county office that keeps your farm records.</p>

<p>An eligible natural disaster includes:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Damaging weather, such as drought, freeze, hail, excessive moisture or wind, or hurricanes.</li>
	<li>An event such as an earthquake or flood.</li>
	<li>A condition related to a natural event, such as excessive heat, plant disease, volcanic smog (VOG), insect infestation.</li>
	<li>Any combination of these conditions.</li>
</ul>

<p>The disaster must directly affect your crop and occur:</p>

<ul>
	<li>During the coverage period, and</li>
	<li>Before or during harvest.</li>
</ul>

<p>NAP provides basic coverage equal to a catastrophic level risk protection plan where the loss:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Exceeds 50% of the expected yield, and</li>
	<li>Is 55% of the average market price.</li>
</ul>

<p>Buy-up coverage is also available in ranges between:</p>

<ul>
	<li>50% to 65% of the yield, in 5 percent increments, and</li>
	<li>100% of the average market price.</li>
</ul>

<p>Other terms and conditions apply.</p>
<p><strong>Application Process</strong></p><p>You must apply for coverage of non-insurable crops using Form CCC-471 NAP BP, <a href="http://www.fsa.usda.gov/Internet/FSA_File/ccc_471_nap_bp.pdf" target="_blank">Application for Coverage</a> (PDF, 141 KB) at your local FSA office, and pay any service fees that apply. You must also file by the application closing date set by your state FSA committee.</p>
<p><strong>Program Contact Information</strong></p><p>Contact your local <a href="http://offices.sc.egov.usda.gov/locator/app?state=us&amp;agency=fsa" target="_blank">FSA office</a> to learn more or get the application closing dates and coverage periods.</p>
<a class="read_less" href="javascript:void(0);">Read Less</a></div></div><div class="row even "><h4 class="program_title">Crop Insurance</h4><p class="agency"><strong>Managing Agency: </strong>U.S. Department of Agriculture</p><div class="program_description_intro"><strong>Program Description: </strong>Crop Insurance protects agricultural producers against crop losses due to natural perils. The program, administered by the U.S. Department of Agriculture's Risk Management... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Crop Insurance" data-agency="U.S. Department of Agriculture">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>Crop Insurance protects agricultural producers against crop losses due to natural perils. The program, administered by the U.S. Department of Agriculture's Risk Management Agency (USDA RMA), offers several plans for crops and livestock. Availability and plans vary by state and county.</p>

<p>You can learn about <a href="http://www.rma.usda.gov/help/faq/basics.html" target="_blank">Crop Insurance Basics</a> under the <a href="http://www.rma.usda.gov/help/faq/" target="_blank">Frequently Asked Questions</a>.</p>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p>To qualify for this program, you must meet the following conditions:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Be an agricultural farmer or rancher.</li>
	<li>Buy a policy for your specific crop(s) by the sales closing date in your county</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Application Process</strong></p><p>To find insurance companies and agents offering crop insurance, visit the <a href="https://www3.rma.usda.gov/tools/agents/companies/" target="_blank">RMA Agent Locator</a>.</p>
<p><strong>Program Contact Information</strong></p><p>If you have questions, get contacts for your local RMA office from the <a href="http://www.rma.usda.gov/aboutrma/fields/rsos.html" target="_blank">Regional Office State Directory</a>. You can also visit the <a href="http://www.rma.usda.gov/" target="_blank">USDA Risk Management Agency</a> website to learn more and find plans in your area.</p>
<a class="read_less" href="javascript:void(0);">Read Less</a></div></div><div class="row odd "><h4 class="program_title">Rural Housing Loans</h4><p class="agency"><strong>Managing Agency: </strong>U.S. Department of Agriculture</p><div class="program_description_intro"><strong>Program Description: </strong>A direct or guaranteed housing loan may be able to help those with low income get a decent, safe, and healthy home in an eligible rural area.

The Direct Loan... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Rural Housing Loans" data-agency="U.S. Department of Agriculture">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>A direct or guaranteed housing loan may be able to help those with low income get a decent, safe, and healthy home in an eligible rural area.</p>

<p>The Direct Loan Program offers a subsidy to help reduce your mortgage payments for a short time. Your family income determines the amount of the subsidy. The Guaranteed Loan Program offers approved lenders a 90% loan note guarantee. This reduces the risk of extending 100% loans to eligible rural buyers.</p>

<p>You may use these loans to help you buy, build, repair, improve, or relocate your primary home.You may also use funds to buy and prepare sites, including water and sewer.</p>

<p>Loans may be available if you live in the U.S., Puerto Rico, U.S. Virgin Islands, Guam, American Samoa, Northern Mariana islands, and Pacific Trust Territories.</p>

<p>For more details, visit the program pages below:</p>

<ul>
	<li><a href="http://www.rd.usda.gov/programs-services/single-family-housing-guaranteed-loan-program" target="_blank">Single Family Housing Guaranteed Loan Program</a></li>
	<li><a href="http://www.rd.usda.gov/programs-services/single-family-housing-direct-home-loans" target="_blank">Single Family Direct Home Loan Program</a></li>
</ul>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p>To qualify for these loans, your home must be in an eligible rural area. You can go to the <a href="http://eligibility.sc.egov.usda.gov/eligibility/welcomeAction.do?NavKey=home@1" target="_blank">USDA Property Eligibility Site</a> to check your address.</p>

<p>Your income must also be within one of the levels below:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Very low - Below 50 percent of the area median income (AMI),</li>
	<li>Low - Between 50 and 80 percent of AMI, or</li>
	<li>Moderate - Below 115 percent of AMI.</li>
</ul>

<p>See <a href="http://www.rd.usda.gov/files/RD-DirectLimitMap.pdf" target="_blank">income limits</a> (PDF, 5 MB) to learn more.</p>

<p>To apply, you must meet the following conditions:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Be without decent, safe, and sanitary housing.</li>
	<li>Not be able to get a loan elsewhere for fair terms and conditions.</li>
	<li>Agree to live in the home as your primary home.</li>
	<li>Be able to take on a legal loan obligation.</li>
	<li>Be a U.S. citizen or eligible noncitizen.</li>
	<li>Not be barred from taking part in federal programs.</li>
</ul>

<p>The home must also meet the conditions below:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Be modest in size for the area.</li>
	<li>Meet the market value loan limit for the area.</li>
	<li>Not have an in-ground swimming pool.</li>
	<li>Not be designed for business use.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Application Process</strong></p><p>To learn more, contact your local <a href="http://offices.sc.egov.usda.gov/locator/app?state=us&amp;agency=rd" target="_blank">USDA Rural Development field office</a>.</p>

<p>To apply for direct loans, you need to complete the forms below:</p>

<ul>
	<li><a href="http://forms.sc.egov.usda.gov/efcommon/eFileServices/eForms/RD410-4.PDF" target="_blank">Uniform Residential Loan Application (RD 410-4)</a> (PDF, 488 KB), and</li>
	<li><a href="http://forms.sc.egov.usda.gov/efcommon/eFileServices/eForms/RD3550-1.PDF" target="_blank">Authorization to Release Information (RD 3550-1)</a> (PDF, 97 KB)</li>
</ul>

<p>To apply for a guaranteed loan, you must contact an approved lender. A <a href="http://eligibility.sc.egov.usda.gov/eligibility/welcomeAction.do?pageAction=GetRHContact&amp;NavKey=contact@12" target="_blank">Guaranteed Loan Contact</a> can help you get information about the approved lenders in your state.</p>
<p><strong>Program Contact Information</strong></p><p>Contact your <a href="http://www.rd.usda.gov/contact-us/state-offices" target="_blank">Rural Development state office</a> to learn more or if you have questions.</p>
<a class="read_less" href="javascript:void(0);">Read Less</a></div></div><div class="row even "><h4 class="program_title">Single Family Housing: Housing Repair Loans and Grants</h4><p class="agency"><strong>Managing Agency: </strong>U.S. Department of Agriculture</p><div class="program_description_intro"><strong>Program Description: </strong>The Single Family Housing Repair Loans and Grants program, also known as the Section 504 Home Repair program, offers loans and grants to elderly and very-low-income... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Single Family Housing: Housing Repair Loans and Grants" data-agency="U.S. Department of Agriculture">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>The Single Family Housing Repair Loans and Grants program, also known as the Section 504 Home Repair program, offers loans and grants to elderly and very-low-income homeowners. Very low income is below 50 percent of the area median income.</p>

<p><strong>How may I use the funds?</strong></p>

<ul>
	<li>Use loan funds to repair, improve, or modernize your home, or remove health and safety hazards.</li>
	<li>Use grant funds only to remove health and safety hazards.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>How much money can I get?</strong></p>

<ul>
	<li>Maximum loan is $20,000.</li>
	<li>Maximum grant is $7,500.</li>
	<li>You may be able to combine loan and grants for up to $27,500.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>What are the terms of the loan or grant?</strong></p>

<ul>
	<li>You can repay loans over 20 years.</li>
	<li>The fixed interest rate for the loan is 1%.</li>
	<li>Loans of $7,500 or more require full title service.</li>
	<li>Grants have a lifetime limit of $7,500.</li>
	<li>You must repay grants if you sell the property in less than 3 years.</li>
	<li>You may be able to get a loan and grant combination if you can repay part but not all of the cost.</li>
</ul>

<p>To learn more, visit one of the program pages below:</p>

<ul>
	<li><a href="http://www.rd.usda.gov/programs-services/single-family-housing-repair-loans-grants" target="_blank">Single Family Housing Repair Loans and Grants</a></li>
	<li><a href="http://www.rd.usda.gov/programs-services/programs-services-individuals" target="_blank">Programs and Services for Individuals</a></li>
</ul>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p>To qualify for the loan program, you must meet all of the conditions below:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Be a homeowner who has very low income,</li>
	<li>Be a U.S. citizen or permanent resident, and</li>
	<li>Live in a rural area; check the address on the <a href="http://eligibility.sc.egov.usda.gov/eligibility/welcomeAction.do?pageAction=sfp&amp;NavKey=property@11" target="_blank">Property Eligibility</a> page.</li>
</ul>

<p>To qualify for the grant program, you must meet the following conditions:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Meet the conditions above,</li>
	<li>Be age 62 or older, and</li>
	<li>Not be able to repay a repair loan.</li>
</ul>

<p>You must also occupy the home and be unable to get affordable credit elsewhere.</p>

<p>See <a href="http://www.rd.usda.gov/files/RD-DirectLimitMap.pdf" target="_blank">income limits</a> (PDF, 5 MB) for more details.</p>
<p><strong>Application Process</strong></p><p>To apply for a loan or grant, you may:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Visit <a href="http://www.sc.egov.usda.gov/" target="_blank">U.S. Department of Agriculture (USDA) Online Services</a>.</li>
	<li>Contact your <a href="http://offices.sc.egov.usda.gov/locator/app?state=us&amp;agency=rd" target="_blank">state's Rural Development field office</a>.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Program Contact Information</strong></p><p>If you have questions, <a href="http://www.rd.usda.gov/browse-state" target="_blank">browse by state</a> to find a USDA home loan specialist in your area.</p>
<a class="read_less" href="javascript:void(0);">Read Less</a></div></div><div class="row odd "><h4 class="program_title">Disaster Legal Services (DLS)</h4><p class="agency"><strong>Managing Agency: </strong>U.S. Department of Homeland Security/FEMA</p><div class="program_description_intro"><strong>Program Description: </strong>Disaster Legal Services (DLS) provides free legal help to low-income disaster survivors. Those who aren't able to get adequate legal services to help with disaster-related... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Disaster Legal Services (DLS)" data-agency="U.S. Department of Homeland Security/FEMA">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>Disaster Legal Services (DLS) provides free legal help to low-income disaster survivors. Those who aren't able to get adequate legal services to help with disaster-related needs.</p>

<p>FEMA provides this service through an agreement with the Young Lawyers Division of the American Bar Association. Their advice is limited to cases that will not generate a fee.</p>

<p>For cases that may generate a fee, DLS turns them over to the local lawyer referral service.</p>

<p>DLS can help with the following:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Insurance claims for medical bills, loss of property, loss of life</li>
	<li>New wills, powers of attorney, and other legal papers lost during the disaster</li>
	<li>Home-repair contracts and contractors</li>
	<li>Problems with landlords</li>
	<li>Proof of home ownership</li>
	<li>FEMA appeals</li>
</ul>

<p>DLS attorneys are not FEMA employees. Their services are confidential and they do not share information with FEMA.</p>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p>To qualify for DLS, you must be a low-income survivor of a federally declared disaster.</p>
<p><strong>Application Process</strong></p><p>You can be referred to DLS by calling:</p>

<ul>
	<li>1-800-621-FEMA (3362)</li>
	<li>TTY 1-800-462-7585</li>
	<li>711 and VRS 1-800-621-3362</li>
</ul>

<p>When you call, you'll get disaster-specific help and information. You'll also learn how to get other legal help.</p>
<p><strong>Program Contact Information</strong></p><p>To learn more, visit the American Bar Association <a href="https://www.americanbar.org/groups/committees/disaster/disaster_relief.html" name="U.S. Department of Homeland Security" target="_blank">Disaster Relief</a> page and the pages below:</p>

<p><a href="https://www.fema.gov/media-library/assets/documents/24413" name="U.S. Department of Homeland Security" target="_blank">Disaster Legal Services Fact Sheet</a></p>

<p><a href="https://www.americanbar.org/groups/committees/disaster/resources/disaster_legal_hotlines.html" name="U.S. Department of Homeland Security" target="_blank">Disaster Legal Hotlines</a></p>

<p><a href="http://www.disasterlegalaid.org/" name="U.S. Department of Homeland Security" target="_blank">National Disaster Legal Aid</a></p>
<a class="read_less" href="javascript:void(0);">Read Less</a></div></div><div class="row even "><h4 class="program_title">Disaster Unemployment Assistance</h4><p class="agency"><strong>Managing Agency: </strong>U.S. Department of Labor</p><div class="program_description_intro"><strong>Program Description: </strong>The Disaster Unemployment Assistance (DUA) program provides temporary benefits to people whose employment or self-employment has been lost or interrupted due to a major... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Disaster Unemployment Assistance" data-agency="U.S. Department of Labor">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>The Disaster Unemployment Assistance (DUA) program provides temporary benefits to people whose employment or self-employment has been lost or interrupted due to a major disaster.</p>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p><strong>Can I get help from the program?</strong></p>

<p>To qualify for DUA you must meet both of the conditions below:</p>

<ol>
	<li>Your job must have been lost or interrupted due to a presidentially declared disaster, and</li>
	<li value="2">You must <em>not</em> be eligible for regular unemployment insurance benefits.</li>
</ol>

<p>If you lived, worked, or were scheduled to work in the declared disaster area, you may qualify for assistance if you meet any of the following conditions:</p>

<ul>
	<li>No longer have a job or place to work.</li>
	<li>Cant reach your job site.</li>
	<li>Cant work because of damage to the job site.</li>
	<li>Were about to start a new job but, due to the disaster, the job no longer exists.</li>
	<li>Cant work because of an injury caused by the disaster.</li>
	<li>Became the major support for a household because the head of household died due to the disaster.</li>
</ul>

<p>You must be available and able to work, unless you meet one of these two conditions:</p>

<ul>
	<li>You have an injury caused by the disaster, or</li>
	<li>You are taking steps to return to self-employment.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Application Process</strong></p><p><strong>How do I file a claim?</strong></p>

<p>After a disaster, your affected state will publish information about DUA availability. As soon as possible, contact your states unemployment agency to file a claim for benefits. You can use the <a href="http://www.careeronestop.org/localhelp/UnemploymentBenefits/find-unemployment-benefits.aspx" target="_blank">CareerOneStop Unemployment Benefits Finder</a> to find the state agency you need.</p>

<p>In some states, you can file online or by phone.</p>

<p>If you evacuated or moved to another state, file a claim in the state where the disaster occurred, or you may contact the agency in the state youre living in for claim filing help.</p>

<p>Visit the U.S. Department of Labors <a href="http://workforcesecurity.doleta.gov/unemploy/disaster.asp" target="_blank">DUA page</a> to learn more.</p>
<p><strong>Program Contact Information</strong></p><p>If you have questions, please call the Employment and Training Helpline for more details.</p>

<ul>
	<li>1-877-US2-JOBS (1-877-872-5627)</li>
	<li>TTY 1-877-889-5627</li>
</ul>
<a class="read_less" href="javascript:void(0);">Read Less</a></div></div><div class="row odd "><h4 class="program_title">Temporary Assistance for Needy Families (TANF)</h4><p class="agency"><strong>Managing Agency: </strong>U.S. Department of Health and Human Services</p><div class="program_description_intro"><strong>Program Description: </strong>The Temporary Assistance for Needy Families (TANF) program helps needy families become self-sufficient. States are given block grants to design and run programs that... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Temporary Assistance for Needy Families (TANF)" data-agency="U.S. Department of Health and Human Services">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>The Temporary Assistance for Needy Families (TANF) program helps needy families become self-sufficient. States are given block grants to design and run programs that fulfill one of the four purposes of TANF:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Provide help to families so children can be cared for in their own homes.</li>
	<li>Reduce the parents dependency by promoting job preparation, work, and marriage.</li>
	<li>Prevent and reduce out-of-wedlock pregnancies.</li>
	<li>Encourage two-parent families.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p>To qualify, you must either be pregnant or responsible for a child under age 19.<br />
You and your qualified child must be one of the following:</p>

<ul>
	<li>U.S. citizen,</li>
	<li>Non-citizen national, or</li>
	<li>Qualified alien.</li>
</ul>

<p>You must also be in one of the categories below:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Low income and under-employed (working for very low wages), or</li>
	<li>Unemployed or about to become unemployed.</li>
</ul>

<p>Check with the TANF agency in your area to learn if you qualify.</p>

<ul>
	<li>Each state decides the benefits it provides.</li>
	<li>Each state sets the criteria you must meet to get benefits and services.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Application Process</strong></p><p>Visit the <a href="https://www.acf.hhs.gov/programs/ofa/help" target="_blank">Help for Families</a> page to get application information for your state, territory, or tribe.</p>
<p><strong>Program Contact Information</strong></p><p>To learn more about this program, visit the<a href="https://www.acf.hhs.gov/programs/ofa/programs/tanf" target="_blank">Temporary Assistance for Needy Families (TANF)</a>page.</p>

It also offers disability benefits... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Public Safety Officers' Benefits Program" data-agency="U.S. Department of Justice">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>The Public Safety Officers' Benefits Program (PSOB) offers death and education benefits to survivors of fallen public safety officers. It also offers disability benefits to officers permanently injured in the line of duty. This includes the officers below:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Law enforcement officers</li>
	<li>Firefighters</li>
	<li>Other first responders</li>
</ul>

<p>The program is an effort of the U.S. Department of Justice, along with:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Local, state, and federal public safety agencies</li>
	<li>National organizations</li>
</ul>

<p>We assign benefit amounts annually and they may vary year to year. This may include a one-time payment for death or disability in the line of duty.</p>

<ul>
	<li>Death that was a direct result of injury on or after September 29, 1976. (Certain fatal heart attacks and strokes are also covered.)</li>
	<li>Disability that was the result of a catastrophic injury on or after November 29, 1990. You must be permanently unable to work.</li>
</ul>

<p>See the <a href="https://www.bja.gov/Publications/PSOB_FS.pdf" target="_blank">Bureau of Justice Assistance (BJA) Fact Sheet</a> (PDF, 944 KB) for details.</p>

<p>Your survivors may also qualify for a monthly educational allowance. This provides support for higher education if you die or are permanently disabled. We base the amount of this benefit on the students status, whether full- or part-time.</p>

<p>See the <a href="https://www.bja.gov/Programs/PSOB/PSOB_Education.pdf" target="_blank">Education Assistance Program</a> (PDF, 1.1 MB) fact sheet for details.</p>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p>Survivors may include any of the following:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Spouses</li>
	<li>Children</li>
	<li>Designated PSOB beneficiaries</li>
	<li>Surviving parents</li>
</ul>

<p>Children may qualify if, at the time death or disability, they are:</p>

<ul>
	<li>A natural, out-of-wedlock, adopted child or stepchild, age 18 or younger.</li>
	<li>A child between 19 and 22 and a full-time student.</li>
	<li>A disabled child over 18 who is unable to support themselves.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Application Process</strong></p><p>Find benefit amounts and how to file claims on the BJA <a href="https://psob.bja.ojp.gov/" target="_blank">Public Safety Officers Benefits Programs</a> Home page.</p>

<a class="read_less" href="javascript:void(0);">Read Less</a></div></div><div class="row even "><h4 class="program_title">Home and Property Disaster Loans</h4><p class="agency"><strong>Managing Agency: </strong>U.S. Small Business Administration</p><div class="program_description_intro"><strong>Program Description: </strong>The U.S. Small Business Administration (SBA) offers affordable financial help to homeowners and renters in declared disaster areas. You don't need to own a business. Help... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Home and Property Disaster Loans" data-agency="U.S. Small Business Administration">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>The U.S. Small Business Administration (SBA) offers affordable financial help to homeowners and renters in declared disaster areas. You don't need to own a business. Help is available in the form of low-interest, long-term loans for losses not fully covered by insurance or other means.</p>

<p>You may borrow up to $200,000 to repair or replace your primary home to its pre-disaster condition. But you can't use the loan to upgrade or add on to the home, unless required by building authority or code.</p>

<p>In some cases, SBA may be able to refinance all or part of a previous mortgage (not to exceed $200,000) if you meet the conditions below:</p>

<ul>
	<li>You can't have credit available elsewhere (as SBA determines).</li>
	<li>Your must have substantially damaged property (as SBA determines).</li>
	<li>You intend to repair or replace the damaged property.</li>
</ul>

<p>SBA considers refinancing when processing each application. They may also be able to increase the loan up to 20 percent of the confirmed physical losses (not to exceed $200,000). You could use the increase to make improvements that may help protect your home from future disasters. Examples of improvements include retaining walls, seawalls, sump pumps, safe rooms, and storm shelters.</p>

<p>Second homes or vacation properties are not eligible. Qualified rental properties may be eligible for assistance under the business disaster loan program.</p>

<p>You may be able to borrow up to $40,000 to replace damaged or destroyed personal property. This may include the following:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Clothing</li>
	<li>Furniture</li>
	<li>Appliances</li>
	<li>Cars</li>
	<li>Other personal property; not real estate or part of the actual structure</li>
</ul>

<p>You may <em>not</em> use the loan to replace extremely expensive or irreplaceable items. This may include the items below:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Antiques</li>
	<li>Collections</li>
	<li>Pleasure boats</li>
	<li>Recreational vehicles</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p>To qualify for SBA disaster assistance, you must have physical damage to your primary home in a declared county.</p>
<p><strong>Application Process</strong></p><p>If youre a homeowner or renter, you must first apply with FEMA.</p>

<p>You may apply to FEMA online on <a href="/" target="_blank">DisasterAssistance.gov</a>.</p>

<p>If you want to apply by phone, please call the FEMA Helpline:</p>

<ul>
	<li>1-800-621-FEMA (3362)</li>
	<li>TTY 1-800-462-7585</li>
	<li>711 or VRS 1-800-621-3362</li>
</ul>

<p>To apply for an SBA disaster loan, you may apply online at any time using the SBA's <a href="https://disasterloan.sba.gov/ela" target="_blank">Disaster Loan Application</a>.</p>

<p>To get personal, one-on-one help from an SBA representative, you may also apply in person at one of the centers below:</p>

<ul>
	<li><a href="https://egateway.fema.gov/ESF6/DRCLocator" target="_blank">FEMA Disaster Recovery Center</a> (DRC)</li>
	<li>SBA Disaster Loan Outreach Center</li>
</ul>

<p>To find a center near you, or for help to apply by mail, contact our Customer Service Center.</p>

<p>If you prefer to mail your application to SBA, please use the following address:</p>

<p style="margin-left: 40px">Processing and Disbursement Center<br />
14925 Kingsport Road<br />
Fort Worth, Texas 76155</p>
<p><strong>Program Contact Information</strong></p><p>If you have questions about the program or on how to apply with SBA, or if you want to find an SBA disaster center near you, contact our Customer Service Center:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Call 1-800-659-2955</li>
	<li>TTY 1-800-877-8339, or</li>
	<li>Email <a href="mailto:disastercustomerservice@sba.gov">disastercustomerservice@sba.gov</a>.</li>
</ul>

<p>You may also visit the SBA <a href="http://www.sba.gov/category/navigation-structure/loans-grants/small-business-loans/disaster-loans" target="_blank">Disaster Loans</a> page to learn more.</p>
<a class="read_less" href="javascript:void(0);">Read Less</a></div></div><div class="row odd "><h4 class="program_title">Business Disaster Loans</h4><p class="agency"><strong>Managing Agency: </strong>U.S. Small Business Administration</p><div class="program_description_intro"><strong>Program Description: </strong>The U.S. Small Business Administration (SBA) offers affordable financial help to businesses and private non-profit organizations in declared disaster areas. Help is... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Business Disaster Loans" data-agency="U.S. Small Business Administration">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>The U.S. Small Business Administration (SBA) offers affordable financial help to businesses and private non-profit organizations in declared disaster areas. Help is available in the form of low-interest, long-term loans for losses not fully covered by insurance or other means.</p>

<p>SBA's disaster loans are the main federal assistance offered for the repair and rebuilding of non-farm, private sector disaster losses. This is the only SBA direct loan program and it is not limited to small businesses.</p>

<p>Businesses of all sizes as well as private non-profit organizations may borrow up to $2 million to repair or replace:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Damaged or destroyed real estate</li>
	<li>Machinery and equipment</li>
	<li>Inventory and other business assets</li>
</ul>

<p>In some cases, SBA may be able to refinance all or part of a prior mortgage or lien. They may also be able to increase the loan up to 20 percent of the confirmed physical losses. You could use the increase to make improvements that reduce the risk of damage by future disasters. Examples of improvements include retaining walls, seawalls, sump pumps, safe rooms, and storm shelters.</p>

<p>The SBA offers Economic Injury Disaster Loans (EIDL) up to $2 million to help meet working capital needs caused by the disaster. Any of the following may qualify for EIDL:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Small businesses</li>
	<li>Small agricultural cooperatives</li>
	<li>Small businesses engaged in aquaculture</li>
	<li>Most private non-profit organizations of all sizes</li>
</ul>

<p>EIDL help is available whether the business had any physical property damage or not.</p>

<p>The statutory limit for business loans is $2 million. This applies to the combination of all funding paid to a business and its affiliates for each disaster.</p>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p>To qualify, your business or private, non-profit organization must have physical damage or economic harm and be located in a declared county.</p>
<p><strong>Application Process</strong></p><p>If you're a homeowner or renter and want to apply for SBA assistance, you must first apply with FEMA.</p>

<p>You may apply to FEMA online on <a href="/" target="_blank">DisasterAssistance.gov</a>.</p>

<p>If you want to apply by phone, you may call the FEMA Helpline:</p>

<ul>
	<li>1-800-621-FEMA (3362)</li>
	<li>TTY 1-800-462-7585</li>
	<li>711 or VRS 1-800-621-3362</li>
</ul>

<p>To apply with SBA, you may apply online at any time using SBA's <a href="https://disasterloan.sba.gov/ela/" target="_blank">Disaster Loan Application</a>.</p>

<p>To get personal, one-on-one help from an SBA representative, you may also apply in person at one of the centers below:</p>

<ul>
	<li><a href="https://egateway.fema.gov/ESF6/DRCLocator" target="_blank">FEMA Disaster Recovery Center</a> (DRC)</li>
	<li>SBA Disaster Loan Outreach Center</li>
	<li>SBA Business Recovery Center</li>
</ul>

<p>To find a center near you, or for help to apply by mail, contact our Customer Service Center.</p>

<p>If you prefer to mail your application to SBA, please use the following address:</p>

<p style="margin-left: 40px">Processing and Disbursement Center<br />
14925 Kingsport Road<br />
Fort Worth, Texas 76155</p>
<p><strong>Program Contact Information</strong></p><p>If you have questions on how to apply with SBA or want to find an SBA disaster center near you, contact our Customer Service Center:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Call 1-800-659-2955</li>
	<li>TTY 1-800-877-8339, or</li>
	<li>Email <a href="mailto:disastercustomerservice@sba.gov">disastercustomerservice@sba.gov</a></li>
</ul>

<p>You may also visit the SBA <a href="http://www.sba.gov/category/navigation-structure/loans-grants/small-business-loans/disaster-loans" target="_blank">Disaster Loans</a> page to learn more.</p>
<a class="read_less" href="javascript:void(0);">Read Less</a></div></div><div class="row even "><h4 class="program_title">Social Security Child's Insurance Benefits</h4><p class="agency"><strong>Managing Agency: </strong>U.S. Social Security Administration</p><div class="program_description_intro"><strong>Program Description: </strong>A child may be able to get Child's Insurance Benefits if one or both of their parents are disabled, retired, or deceased. Under certain circumstances, the following... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Social Security Child's Insurance Benefits" data-agency="U.S. Social Security Administration">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>A child may be able to get Child's Insurance Benefits if one or both of their parents are disabled, retired, or deceased. Under certain circumstances, the following children may also qualify for benefits:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Stepchild</li>
	<li>Grandchild</li>
	<li>Step-grandchild, or</li>
	<li>Adopted child.</li>
</ul>

<p>Read <a href="https://www.ssa.gov/pubs/EN-05-10085.pdf" target="_blank">Benefits for Children</a> (PDF, 159 KB) for more details.</p>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p>A child must have one of the following to qualify for benefits:</p>

<ul>
	<li>A parent who is entitled to Social Security retirement or disability benefits, or</li>
	<li>A parent who died after earning enough Social Security credits on their record.</li>
</ul>

<p>The child must also meet the conditions below:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Be unmarried,</li>
	<li>Be younger than age 18, or</li>
	<li>Be age 18-19 and a full-time student (no higher than grade 12), or</li>
	<li>Be age 18 or older and disabled. (The disability must have begun before age 22).</li>
</ul>

<a class="read_less" href="javascript:void(0);">Read Less</a></div></div><div class="row even "><h4 class="program_title">Social Security Lump Sum Death Payment</h4><p class="agency"><strong>Managing Agency: </strong>U.S. Social Security Administration</p><div class="program_description_intro"><strong>Program Description: </strong>Are you the surviving spouse or care for the child of a worker who died? If so, you or the child(ren) may get a special lump-sum death payment of $255 if you or the... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Social Security Lump Sum Death Payment" data-agency="U.S. Social Security Administration">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>Are you the surviving spouse or care for the child of a worker who died? If so, you or the child(ren) may get a special lump-sum death payment of $255 if you or the child(ren) meet certain conditions.</p>

<p>For more details, visit the <a href="https://www.ssa.gov/planners/survivors/ifyou7.html" target="_blank">Survivors Planner: A Special Lump-sum Death Payment</a> page.</p>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p>In most cases, you can get a lump-sum death payment if you were living in the same household when your spouse died. If you were living apart, you may still get paid if, during the month they died, you met the conditions below:</p>

<ul>
	<li>You were already getting benefits on their record; or</li>
	<li>You became eligible for benefits on their record upon their death.</li>
</ul>

<p>If there's no eligible surviving spouse, a child may get the payment if, during the month the worker died, they met the conditions below:</p>

<ul>
	<li>They were already getting benefits on the worker's record; or</li>
	<li>They became eligible for benefits upon the worker's death.</li>
</ul>

<p>If you or a surviving child does not currently get benefits, you must apply for this payment within two years of the date of death.</p>
<p><strong>Application Process</strong></p><p>Visit the <a href="https://www.ssa.gov/forms/ssa-8.html" target="_blank">Information You Need to Apply For Lump-sum Death Benefit  Form SSA-8</a> for details on how to apply.</p>

<p>If you would like to find out what other Social Security Administration (SSA) benefits you may qualify for, use <a href="http://ssabest.benefits.gov/" target="_blank">SSA Benefit Eligibility Screening Tool (BEST)</a> on Benefits.gov. When you complete the questionnaire, you get a list of benefits to review. You can print this page for your records.</p>

<p>When you know which benefits you may apply for, click <a href="https://www.ssa.gov/forms/apply-for-benefits.html" target="_blank">Apply for Social Security Benefits</a> to apply online. You can also call the phone numbers below to learn more about SSA benefits and how to apply.</p>

	<li>TTY 1-800-325-0778</li>

<a class="read_less" href="javascript:void(0);">Read Less</a></div></div><div class="row odd "><h4 class="program_title">Social Security Mother's or Father's Insurance Benefits</h4><p class="agency"><strong>Managing Agency: </strong>U.S. Social Security Administration</p><div class="program_description_intro"><strong>Program Description: </strong>Are you the surviving spouse or surviving divorced spouse of an insured worker who died? Are you also caring for the workers child? If so, you may be able to get Social... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Social Security Mother's or Father's Insurance Benefits" data-agency="U.S. Social Security Administration">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>Are you the surviving spouse or surviving divorced spouse of an insured worker who died? Are you also caring for the workers child? If so, you may be able to get Social Security Mother's or Father's Insurance Benefits.</p>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p>As a surviving spouse or surviving divorced spouse, you must meet the conditions below to qualify:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Be the widow(er) of an insured worker or, if divorced, be unmarried.</li>
	<li>Meet the marriage duration requirement.</li>
	<li>Care for the workers child who is one of the following:
	<ul>
		<li>Under age 16, or</li>
		<li>Disabled and entitled to child's insurance benefits on their record.</li>
	</ul>
	</li>
</ul>

<p>If youre a surviving divorced mother or father, the child in your care must be the workers natural or legally adopted child who is entitled to the childs benefits. You must also meet the conditions below:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Have a final divorce decree.</li>
	<li>Be entitled to a lower Social Security retirement benefit on your own record.</li>
	<li>Not be entitled to a widow(er)s benefit.</li>
</ul>

<p>Other terms and conditions also apply. You can get more information through the links provided below.</p>

	You served in the active U.S. military from... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Social Security Special Benefits for Qualified WWII Veterans" data-agency="U.S. Social Security Administration">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>Certain World War II veterans can get special benefits if they served in one of the two groups below:</p>

<ul>
	<li>You served in the active U.S. military from September 16, 1940 through July 24, 1947.</li>
	<li>You are Filipino and served in the organized military of the Philippines from July 26, 1941 through December 30, 1946. (While those forces were in the service of the U.S. Armed Forces).</li>
</ul>

<p>Read <a href="https://www.ssa.gov/pubs/EN-05-10157.pdf" target="_blank">Special Benefits for Certain World War II Veterans</a> (PDF, 107 KB) to learn more.</p>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p>To qualify for benefits, you must meet all of the conditions below:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Live outside of the U.S.</li>
	<li>Be age 65 or older as of December 14, 1999.</li>
	<li>Be a World War II veteran from one of the groups above.</li>
	<li>Qualify for Supplemental Security Income (SSI) as of December 1999.</li>
	<li>Qualify for SSI the month you apply for these benefits.</li>
	<li>Have other benefit income thats less than 75 percent of the current SSI rate.</li>
</ul>

<p>Benefits are payable for each month you live outside of the U.S. if you qualify. Dependents and survivors do not qualify for this benefit.</p>

<a class="read_less" href="javascript:void(0);">Read Less</a></div></div><div class="row even "><h4 class="program_title">Supplemental Security Income (SSI)</h4><p class="agency"><strong>Managing Agency: </strong>U.S. Social Security Administration</p><div class="program_description_intro"><strong>Program Description: </strong>Supplemental Security Income (SSI) is a federal income supplement program. General tax revenues fund the program, not Social Security taxes. The program has two... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Supplemental Security Income (SSI)" data-agency="U.S. Social Security Administration">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>Supplemental Security Income (SSI) is a federal income supplement program. General tax revenues fund the program, <em>not</em> Social Security taxes. The program has two main objectives:</p>

<ul>
	<li>To help those who are aged, blind, and disabled, who have little or no income or resources.</li>
	<li>To provide cash to meet basic needs for food, clothing, and shelter.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p>You may qualify for Supplemental Security Income if you meet the conditions below:</p>

<ul>
	<li>You are age 65 or older, blind, or disabled.</li>
	<li>You live in one of the 50 States, the District of Columbia, or the Northern Mariana Islands. Except for a child of military parent(s) assigned to permanent duty anywhere outside the U.S. or certain students temporarily abroad.</li>
	<li>You are a citizen or national of the U.S, or</li>
	<li>You are an alien who meets one of the requirements below:
	<ul>
		<li>You met the alien status requirements for benefits payable starting on August 22, 1996.</li>
		<li>You were a lawful permanent resident of the U.S., or were permanently living in the U.S. under color of law, for benefits payable before August 22, 1996.</li>
	</ul>
	</li>
	<li>You have income and resources within stated limits; and</li>
	<li>You file an application.</li>
</ul>

<p>You may also qualify if you are one of the following:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Under age 18, or</li>
	<li>Under age 22 and a student regularly attending school, college, or training designed to prepare you for a paying job.</li>
</ul>

<p>The spouse of an eligible person may qualify if they also meet all of the conditions above and live in the same household. Both people must file their own application and meet all criteria to prove they are eligible as a couple.</p>

<p>Find answers to common questions about the program from the <a href="https://www.ssa.gov/ssi/index.htm" target="_blank">Supplemental Security Income Home Page</a>.</p>
<p><strong>Application Process</strong></p><p>Visit the <a href="https://www.ssa.gov/ssi/text-apply-ussi.htm" target="_blank">Understanding Supplemental Security Income (SSI) Application Process</a> page for details on how to apply.</p>

<p>We can help you apply for SSI benefits if you make an appointment. You mayeither speak to someone on the phone or meet in person at your local Social Security office. You can also visit the local office without an appointment, but wait times will be longer.</p>

<p>To find out what other Social Security Administration (SSA) benefits you may qualify for, use the <a href="http://ssabest.benefits.gov/" target="_blank">SSA Benefit Eligibility Screening Tool (BEST)</a> on Benefits.gov. When you complete the questionnaire, you get a list of benefits to review. You can print this page for your records.</p>

<p>When you know which benefits you may apply for, click <a href="https://www.ssa.gov/forms/apply-for-benefits.html" target="_blank">Apply for Social Security Benefits</a> to apply online. You can also call the phone numbers below to learn more about SSA benefits and how to apply.</p>
<p><strong>Program Contact Information</strong></p><p>Visit the <a href="https://www.ssa.gov/agency/contact/" target="_blank">Contact Social Security</a> page to view all of our contact options. You can also learn about our online and special services. This includes free interpreter services.</p>

<p>To learn more about Social Security, visit our <a href="https://www.ssa.gov/pubs/" target="_blank">Publications</a> page or call us:</p>

<ul>
	<li>1-800-772-1213</li>
	<li>TTY 1-800-325-0778</li>
</ul>
<a class="read_less" href="javascript:void(0);">Read Less</a></div></div><div class="row odd "><h4 class="program_title">Disaster Assistance and Emergency Relief Program for Individuals and Businesses</h4><p class="agency"><strong>Managing Agency: </strong>U.S. Department of the Treasury</p><div class="program_description_intro"><strong>Program Description: </strong>If you have damaged or lost property in a federally declared disaster area, you may be able to get money back from the IRS right now.

Individuals and businesses... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Disaster Assistance and Emergency Relief Program for Individuals and Businesses" data-agency="U.S. Department of the Treasury">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>If you have damaged or lost property in a federally declared disaster area, you may be able to get money back from the IRS right now.</p>

<p>Individuals and businesses in these areas can get faster refunds by claiming disaster losses on their tax return for the prior year. You can usually do this by filing an amended return.</p>

<p>For some disasters, the IRS may grant extra time to file returns and pay taxes.</p>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p>If your address is in a declared area, you can deduct casualty losses in one of two ways:</p>

<ul>
	<li>On your return in the year of the disaster event, or</li>
	<li>File an amended return to deduct the loss in the year prior to the disaster.</li>
</ul>

<p>You must use <a href="http://www.irs.gov/pub/irs-pdf/f4684.pdf" target="_blank">Form 4684</a> (PDF, 139 KB) to report a gain or deductible loss.</p>

<p>When FEMA authorizes Individual Assistance (IA), the IRS may postpone tax deadlines to give you extra time to file returns and pay federal taxes.</p>
<p><strong>Application Process</strong></p><p>If your IRS taxpayer address of record is in a disaster area declared for FEMA IA, your tax account is auto-coded for the filing and payment relief.<br />
<br />
For an affected taxpayer whose area isnt declared, you must call the IRS to self-identify for disaster relief:</p>

<ul>
	<li>1-866-562-5227</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Program Contact Information</strong></p><p>To learn more, visit <a href="http://www.irs.gov/Businesses/Small-Businesses-&amp;-Self-Employed/Disaster-Assistance-and-Emergency-Relief-for-Individuals-and-Businesses-1" target="_blank">Disaster Assistance and Emergency Relief for Individuals and Businesses</a>. Or you may use the <a href="http://apps.irs.gov/app/officeLocator/index.jsp" target="_blank">Taxpayer Assistance Center Office Locator</a> to find your local center.</p>

<p>You may also visit the <a href="https://www.mymoney.gov/Pages/Hurricane.aspx" target="_blank">Financial Recovery Resources</a> page to find other resources.</p>
<a class="read_less" href="javascript:void(0);">Read Less</a></div></div><div class="row even "><h4 class="program_title">Federal Retiree Benefits - Services Online</h4><p class="agency"><strong>Managing Agency: </strong>U.S. Office of Personnel Management</p><div class="program_description_intro"><strong>Program Description: </strong>OPMs Services Online site offers retirement services on demand to federal annuitants and their survivors. You can use it to perform any of the actions... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="Federal Retiree Benefits - Services Online" data-agency="U.S. Office of Personnel Management">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p>OPMs Services Online site offers retirement services on demand to federal annuitants and their survivors. You can use it to perform any of the actions below:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Change your income tax withholding, mailing address, or password.</li>
	<li>Request a duplicate annuity booklet.</li>
	<li>Set up an allotment to checking, savings, or to an organization.</li>
	<li>Sign up for direct deposit.</li>
	<li>Update your email address or opt-in to get electronic info.</li>
	<li>View or print annuity statement, verification of income, or year-to-date summary of payments.</li>
	<li>Print 1099-R tax forms for the current or past four calendar years.</li>
	<li>View or print a retirement services reference card (ID card).</li>
	<li>View or print verification of life insurance (FEGLI).</li>
	<li>View the status of your case while in interim pay.</li>
</ul>

<p>You cannot use Services Online to make changes to your federal dental or vision insurance (FEDVIP) coverage. Contact <a href="https://www.benefeds.com/" target="_blank">BENEFEDS</a> or call 1-877-888-3337 to make changes or comments related to FEDVIP.</p>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p>You may use Services Online if youre a federal retiree or survivor annuitant under one of the systems below:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Civil Service Retirement System (CSRS),</li>
	<li>Federal Employees Retirement System (FERS) or FERS Special, or</li>
	<li>Organization Retirement and Disability System (ORDS).</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Application Process</strong></p><p>Theres no application for this program. Just visit OPMs <a href="https://www.opm.gov/retirement-services/" target="_blank">Retirement Services</a> page to learn more.</p>
<p><strong>Program Contact Information</strong></p><p>To find all of the retirement info and services offered, visit the <a href="https://www.servicesonline.opm.gov/" target="_blank">Services Online</a> website.</p>

<p>Phone:</p>

<ul>
	<li>1-888-767-6738</li>
	<li>TTY 1-855-887-4957</li>
	<li>Federal Relay Service 1-800-877-8339</li>
</ul>

<p>If youre hearing-impaired, you may use Federal Relay to reach a Communications Assistant (CA). The CA dials the number you need and relays the call between a voice telephone and text telephone (TTY).</p>

<p>Visit the <a href="https://www.federalrelay.us/federal-relay-services" target="_blank">Federal Relay</a> site to find other access numbers.</p>

If you get medical treatment or a benefit payment from the Department of... <a class="read_more questionnaire-foa-read-more" href="javascript:void(0);" data-foa="VA Change of Address" data-agency="U.S. Department of Veterans Affairs">Read More</a></div><div class="program_description" style="display: none"><strong>Program Description: </strong><p><strong><em>Do you need to change your address because of a disaster?</em></strong></p>

<p>If you get medical treatment or a benefit payment from the Department of Veterans Affairs (VA), you may be able to update your address or direct deposit information through the eBenefits website. Or VA may be able to make the change over the phone or help you find the correct address to mail a request to.</p>
<p><strong>General Program Requirements</strong></p><p>To qualify, you must meet one of the conditions below:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Be currently enrolled in the VA medical system and get VA medical treatment or assistance, or</li>
</ul>

<ul>
	<li>Get a benefit payment from VA.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Application Process</strong></p><p>To change your address for VA benefit payments, you can do one of the following:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Update your contact information online using <a href="https://www.ebenefits.va.gov/ebenefits/" target="_blank">eBenefits</a> for compensation, pension, and post-9/11 GI Bill education benefits. You can click <strong>Register</strong> at the top of the page to register for an account.</li>
	<li>Call the VA at 1-800-827-1000 or visit your local VA <a href="http://www.benefits.va.gov/benefits/offices.asp" target="_blank">regional benefit office</a>.</li>
	<li>Send a Request for Change of Address/Cancellation of Direct Deposit form (<a href="http://www.va.gov/vaforms/form_detail.asp?FormNo=20-572">VA Form 20-572</a>) to:</li>
</ul>

<p style="margin-left: 0.5in;">U.S. Department of Veterans Affairs<br />
Claims Intake Center<br />
PO Box 4444<br />
Janesville, WI 53547-4444</p>

<p>If you wish to change your address formedical enrollment or records:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Please contact the VA facility where you get treatment, or</li>
	<li>Call the VA Health Benefits Service at 1-877-222-8387.</li>
</ul>

<p>You may find address and other contact details for your VA medical facility at the <a href="http://www.va.gov/directory/guide/division.asp?dnum=1" target="_blank">Veterans Health Administration (VHA) Locations</a> page.</p>

<p>To apply for other Veterans benefits and view your status, open a free eBenefits Premium account. eBenefits is a one-stop resource for Department of Defense (DoD) and VA benefits and services. Veterans, Servicemembers, and their families may open eBenefits accounts.</p>

<p>With a Premium account you can handle self-service actions like the following:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Check claim status.</li>
	<li>Handle GI Bill enrollment.</li>
	<li>Get copies of civil service preference letters, DD214, and other personal information.</li>
</ul>

<p>Visit <a href="http://www.ebenefits.va.gov/" target="_blank">eBenefits</a> to learn more or register for an account.</p>
